        iphone = (ua.match(/iphone/i) == "iphone"),

        channel = window.location.hostname.split(".")[0],
        loc = window.location;

        loc.href = "http://3g.163.com/touch/@channel@/".replace("@channel@",channel);
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
(function() {
	    var nav_value = {
	        platform : ""
	    };
	    var nav = {
	        detect : function() {
	            if (navigator.platform.indexOf("Win") > -1) {
	                nav_value.platform = "ua-win";
	            } else if (navigator.platform.indexOf("Mac") > -1) {
	                nav_value.platform = "ua-mac";
	            } else if (navigator.platform.indexOf("iPad") > -1 || navigator.platform.indexOf("iPhone") > -1) {
	                nav_value.platform = "ua-ios";
	            } else {
	                return false
	            }
	            ;
	        },
	        init : function() {
	            this.detect();
	            if (nav_value.platform) {
	                $("html").addCss(nav_value.platform);
	            };
	        }
	    };
	    nav.init();
	})();
	
	NTES.ready(function($){
		var App = NTESCommonNavigator.core.Controller,
		    Event = NTESCommonNavigator.core.Event.Base,
		    ModelEvent = NTESCommonNavigator.core.Event.Model, 
		    app = NTESCommonNavigator.utils.app = App();//添加全局登录响应.
			app.bind(Event.DATA_CHANGED, function(data){
			});
			app.bind(ModelEvent.MAIL_INFO_LOADED, function(data){
			});
			app.bind(ModelEvent.WEIBO_INFO_LOADED, function(data){
			});
		app.refresh();
	});
//]]>

(function(){	
	var version = window.navigator.appVersion;
	var isIE6 = (version.indexOf("MSIE 6.0") != -1 || version.indexOf("MSIE 5.5") != -1)? true:false;
	if(location.hostname.indexOf("news") == -1){   
           showQR(460, "http://img2.cache.netease.com/news/2013/newapp5.jpg");
	}
	function showQR(top, imgUrl){
		var QRbox= document.createElement("div");
		var QRboxCSS ={
			'width': "110px",
			'height': "147px",
			'position': "fixed",
			'_position': "absolute",
			'top': top + "px",
			'right': "3px",
			'display':"block",
			'zIndex':100
		};
		for(var key in QRboxCSS){
			QRbox.style[key] = QRboxCSS[key];
		}
	 	if(isIE6){
	 		QRbox.style.position = "absolute";
	 	}
	 	
		QRbox.innerHTML="<a href='http://3g.163.com/links/4102' target='_blank'></a>";
		var link =QRbox.getElementsByTagName("a")[0];
		var linkCSS = {
			display:"block",
			width: "100%",
			height: "100%",
			backgroundImage: "url("+imgUrl+")",
			backgroundPosition: "0px 0px"
		};
		for(var key in linkCSS){
			link.style[key] = linkCSS[key]
		}
		document.body.appendChild(QRbox);
		var linkEventMap = {
			"mouseover": function(){
				link.style.backgroundPosition = "-110px 0px";
			},
			"mouseout": function(){
				link.style.backgroundPosition = "0px 0px";
			}
		}
		for(var evt in linkEventMap){
			var func = linkEventMap[evt];
			addEvent(evt, link, func);
		}
		addEvent("scroll", window, function(){
			if(isIE6){
				QRbox.style.top = getScrollTop() + top + "px";
			}
		})
	}
	function addEvent(evt, elem, callback){
		if(elem.addEventListener){
			elem.addEventListener(evt, callback, false)
		} else {
			elem.attachEvent && elem.attachEvent("on"+evt, callback);
		} 
	}
	function getScrollTop(){
	    if(typeof pageYOffset!= 'undefined'){
	        //most browsers
	        return pageYOffset;
	    }
	    else{
	        var B= document.body; //IE 'quirks'
	        var D= document.documentElement; //IE with doctype
	        D= (D.clientHeight)? D: B;
	        return D.scrollTop;
	    }
	}
})();

<script>
    (function(){
        NTES.ui.PopUpLayer = function(ctrl, content){
            var timerId;
            function show(){
                content.style.display = "block";
                $("#getCalendar").addCss('arrowHover');
            }
            function hide(){
                content.style.display = "none";
                $("#getCalendar").removeCss('arrowHover');
            }
            function delayHide(){
                clearTimer();
                timerId = setTimeout(hide, 300);
            }
            function clearTimer(){
                if (timerId) {
                    clearTimeout(timerId);
                    timerId = null;
                }
            }
            NTES.event.addEvent(ctrl, "click", show);
            NTES.event.addEvent(ctrl, "mouseout", delayHide);
            NTES.event.addEvent(ctrl, "mouseover", clearTimer);
            NTES.event.addEvent(content, "mouseover", clearTimer);
            NTES.event.addEvent(content, "mouseout", delayHide);
        };
        var dayCountInMonths = [31, 28, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31];
        NTES.ui.Calendar = function(year, month){
            this.constructor = arguments.callee;
            this.setDate(year, month);
        };
        NTES.ui.Calendar.prototype = {
            getYear: function(){
                return this._year;
            },
            getMonth: function(){
                return this._month + 1;
            },
            setDate: function(y, m){
                var now = new Date();
                this._year = isNaN(y) ? now.getFullYear() : y;
                this._month = isNaN(m) ? now.getMonth() : m - 1;
            },
            draw: function(tpl){
                var dayCount = NTES.ui.Calendar.getDayCount(this._year, this._month + 1),
                        tool = new Date(this._year, this._month, 1),//new Date(year, month, day, hours, minutes, seconds, microseconds) //时间数值
                        now = new Date(), firstDay = tool.getDay(), data = {
                            year: this._year,
                            month: this._month + 1,
                            weeks: []
                        }, i, state, temp, week = [];
                now.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);//设置指定的时间的小时字段。
                now = now.getTime();
                while (firstDay-- > 0) {
                    week.push({
                        value: ""
                    });
                }
                for (i = 1; i <= dayCount; i++) {
                    tool.setDate(i);
                    temp = tool.getTime();
                    if (temp > now) {
                        state = -1;
                    }
                    else if (temp < now) {
                        state = 1;
                    } else {
                        state = 0;
                    }
                    week.push({
                        value: i,
                        state: state
                    });
                    if (week.length === 7) {
                        data.weeks.push(week);
                        week = [];
                    }
                }
                if (week.length % 7 !== 0) { // 补全后面的空白
                    while (week.length < 7) {
                        week.push({
                            value: ""
                        });
                    }
                    data.weeks.push(week);
                }
                return NTES.util.parseTpl(tpl, data);
            }
        };
        NTES.ui.Calendar.getDayCount = function(y, m){
            return 2 == m ? (0 == y % 4 && 0 != y % 100 || 0 == y % 400 ? 29 : 28) : dayCountInMonths[m - 1];
        };
    })();
    var Template = {
        _cache: {},
        get: function(name){
            return this._cache[name] == null ? "" : this._cache[name];
        },
        parse: function(name, obj){
            return NTES.util.parseTpl(this.get(name), obj);
        },
        init: function(){
            var templates = $("#templates > div"), i = templates.length;
            while (--i >= 0) {
                this._cache[templates[i].className] = templates[i].innerHTML.replace(/(?:^<!--)|(?:-->$)/g, "");
            }
        }
    };
    Template.init();
    var CalendarController = {
        _now: new Date(),
        init: function(){
            var year = this._now.getFullYear(), month = this._now.getMonth() + 1;
            $("#setYear").innerHTML = year;
            $("#setMonth").innerHTML = month;
            //$("#displayDate").innerHTML = String.format("%1月%2日 星期%3", month, this._now.getDate(), "日一二三四五六".charAt(this._now.getDay()));
            this._calendar = new NTES.ui.Calendar(year, month);
            $("#calendarList").innerHTML = this._calendar.draw(Template.get("calendar"));
            $("#preMonth").addEvent("click", function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                $("#nextMonth").removeCss("futureMonth");
                CalendarController.setMonth(-1);
            });
        },
        setMonth: function(relative){
            var year = this._now.getFullYear(), month = this._now.getMonth() + 1 + relative;
            if (month > 12) {
                year++;
                month = month - 12;
            }
            else
            if (month <= 0) {
                year--;
                month = month + 12;
            }
            this._now.setFullYear(year, month - 1);
            $("#setYear").innerHTML = year;
            $("#setMonth").innerHTML = month;
            this._calendar.setDate(year, month);
            $("#calendarList").innerHTML = this._calendar.draw(Template.get("calendar"));
        }
    };
    CalendarController.init();
    //判断选中月和当前月
    $("#nextMonth").addEvent("click", function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var currentYear = currentDate.getFullYear();
        var currentMonth = currentDate.getMonth()+1;
        var tempYear = $("#setYear").innerHTML;
        var tempMonth = $("#setMonth").innerHTML;
        if ((tempYear > currentYear) || (tempYear == currentYear && tempMonth >= currentMonth)) {
            $("#nextMonth").removeCss("futureMonth");
            $("#nextMonth").addCss("futureMonth");
        } else if ((tempYear < currentYear) || (tempYear == currentYear && tempMonth < currentMonth)) {
            CalendarController.setMonth(1);
        } else {
            CalendarController.setMonth(1);
        }
    });
    //
    new NTES.ui.PopUpLayer($("#getCalendar"), $("#calendarBox"));
</script>

var stockSuggest = new ntesStockSuggest({
    // 输入框id
    inputid: "socode",
    // 记录数
    max: 10,
    tooltip: "代码/拼音/名称",
    // 左对齐的元素, 没有则按输入框
    posElem: "selstockinput",
    // 获取查询类型HS/HK/US/...
    getType: function(){
        var sel = document.getElementById("selstockinput");
        return sel.options[sel.selectedIndex].value;
    },
    // 选中某一项
    callback: function(item){
        typeMap = {
            "SH":"http://quotes.money.163.com/0{0}.html",
            "SZ":"http://quotes.money.163.com/1{0}.html",
            "HK":"http://quotes.money.163.com/hkstock/{0}.html",
            "FX":"http://quotes.money.163.com/forex/hq/{0}.html",
            "US":"http://quotes.money.163.com/usstock/hq/{0}.html",
            "FN":"http://quotes.fund.163.com/html/{0}.html",
            "FU":"http://quotes.money.163.com/futures/hq/{0}.html"
        };
        url = typeMap[item["type"]].replace("{0}",  item["symbol"]);
        window.open(url);
    }
});

//IP判断
//return north:北京 east:上海 shenzhen:深圳
var houseIPQuery=new Object();
(function() {
    var china = {
        north : "|北京市|天津市|河北省|山西省|内蒙古|辽宁省|吉林省|黑龙江省|山东省|",
        east : "|上海市|江苏省|浙江省|安徽省|江西省|",
        sichuan : "|四川省|",
        shenzhen : "|深圳市|",
        south : "|广东省|",
        hainan : "|海南省|",
        foshan : "|佛山市|",
        others : "|广州市|"
    };
    var locQuery = {
        url : "http://ipservice.163.com/ipquery",
        cookieName : "locOfCh",
        exec : function(onComplete) {
            //var result = NTES.cookie.get(this.cookieName);
            var result = "";
            if (result != "" && china.hasOwnProperty(result)) {
                onComplete(result);
            } else {
                NTES.ajax.importJs(this.url, function() {
                    if (typeof lo != "undefined" && typeof lc != "undefined") {
                        var tempO = "|" + lo + "|", tempC = "|" + lc + "|";
                        if (china.north.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
                            result = "north";
                        } else if (china.east.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
                            result = "east";
                        } else if (china.shenzhen.indexOf(tempC) != -1) {
                            result = "shenzhen";
                        } else if (china.sichuan.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
                            result = "sichuan";
                        }else if (china.south.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
                            result = "south";
                        } else {
                            result = "others";
                        }
                    }
                    if (result) {
                        //NTES.cookie.set(locQuery.cookieName, result, '1M',".163.com");
                        onComplete(result);
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    };
    houseIPQuery = locQuery;
})();//房产IP定向
houseIPQuery.exec(function(loc){
    //north:北京 east:上海 shenzhen:深圳 others:广州
    if (loc == "north") {
        //        $("#house-bj").style.display = "block";
        $("#house-bj").removeCss("mhidden");
        $("#house-gz").style.display = "none";
    }
    else
    if (loc == "east") {
        $("#house-sh").style.display = "block";
        $("#house-gz").style.display = "none";
    }
    else
    if (loc == "shenzhen") {
        $("#house-sz").style.display = "block";
        $("#house-gz").style.display = "none";
    }
});

var hebeiSiteIPQuery=new Object();
(function() {
    var hebei = "|河北省|";
    var locQuery = {
        url : "http://ipservice.163.com/ipquery",
        cookieName : "locOfHebeiSite",
        exec : function(onComplete) {
            var result = NTES.cookie.get(this.cookieName);
            if (result != "" && hebei.hasOwnProperty(result)) {
                onComplete(result);
            } else {
                NTES.ajax.importJs(this.url, function() {
                    if (typeof lo != "undefined" && typeof lc != "undefined") {
                        var tempO = "|" + lo + "|", tempC = "|" + lc + "|";
                        if (hebei.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
                            result = "hebei";
                        } else {
                            result = "others";
                        }
                    }
                    if (result) {
                        NTES.cookie.set(locQuery.cookieName, result, '1M',".163.com");
                        onComplete(result);
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    };
    hebeiSiteIPQuery = locQuery;
})();//河北站IP定向

        $("#ui-til3-tab-g").style.display = "none";
        $("#ui-til3-tab-o").style.display = "block";
    }
});

<script type="text/javascript">
    //Widget Slide
    /*鼠标放上去出现切换大按钮和缩略图列表*/
    var ctrlTabs = $('.widget-slide-ctrl-tabs');
    var ctrlPrev = $('.widget-slide-ctrl-prev');
    var ctrlNext = $('.widget-slide-ctrl-next');
    var FOCUS_DELAY;
    //页面加载完，再执行图片切换
    $(window).addEvent('load', function(){
        /*鼠标放小切换图上，出现切换图标*/
        $('.widget-slide').addEvent('mouseover',function(){
            clearTimeout(FOCUS_DELAY);
            $( ".widget-slide-ctrl-tabs", $(this)).addCss('visibility:visible;');
            $( ".widget-slide-ctrl-prev", $(this)).addCss('visibility:visible;');//类似于find(),$(selector, abc)
            $( ".widget-slide-ctrl-next",  $(this)).addCss('visibility:visible;');
        }) .addEvent('mouseout',function(){
                    //当前函数没有执行对象，就用一个变量储存当前的this
                    var t = this;
                    FOCUS_DELAY = setTimeout(function(){
                        $( ".widget-slide-ctrl-tabs", $(t)).addCss('visibility:hidden;');
                        $( ".widget-slide-ctrl-prev", $(t)).addCss('visibility:hidden;');
                        $( ".widget-slide-ctrl-next",  $(t)).addCss('visibility:hidden;');
                    }, 25);
                });
        //Mod Scroll
        var Scrl = function(elem){
            var axis = "x";
            if ( $(elem).attr("class").indexOf("mod-scroll-y") != -1 ) axis = "y";
            var t = this, body = NTES.one("> div.widget-slide-body > ul", elem);
            t._ctrls = $("> div.widget-slide-ctrl > ul.widget-slide-ctrl-nav > li", elem);
            t._ctrls_img = $("> div.widget-slide-ctrl > div.widget-slide-ctrl-tabs > ul > li", elem);
            t._len = t._ctrls.length;
            t.index = 0;
            //修复滚动图片不出来bug
            var gsty = NTES.style.getCurrentStyle,
                    onli = NTES.one("> li", body),
                    offWidth = onli.offsetWidth || (parseInt(gsty(onli, "width")) + parseInt(gsty(onli, "padding-left")) + parseInt(gsty(onli, "padding-right")));
            this._elem = elem;
            //
            if (axis == "x"){
                var bWidth = offWidth * body.$("> li").length;
//                var bWidth = NTES.one("> li", body).offsetWidth * body.$("> li").length;
                t._step = bWidth / t._len;
                body.addCss({ width: bWidth + "px"});
                $(body.parentNode).addCss({ width: t._step + "px"});
            }else{
                t._step = NTES.one("> li", body).offsetHeight;
                var bHeight = t._step * t._len;
                body.addCss({ height: bHeight + "px"});
                $(body.parentNode).addCss({ height: t._step + "px"});
            }
            t._scrl = new NTES.ui.Scroll(body, axis);
            if (axis == "y"){
                t._scrl.speed = 50;//50
                t._scrl.fps = 20;//20
                t._scrl.lpf = 1;
            }
            /*鼠标放到切换小按钮，切换大图*/
            t._ctrls.each(function(i){
                $(this).addEvent("mouseover", t.show.bind(t, i), i);
            });
            /*鼠标放到缩略图上，切换大图*/
            t._ctrls_img.each(function(i){
                $(this).addEvent("mouseover", t.show.bind(t, i), i);
            });
            /*鼠标点击左右切换按钮，切换大图*/
            NTES.one("> div.widget-slide-ctrl > a.widget-slide-ctrl-prev", elem).addEvent("click", function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                t.show(--t.index);
            }).addEvent("mouseup", function(){ this.blur(); });
            NTES.one("> div.widget-slide-ctrl > a.widget-slide-ctrl-next", elem).addEvent("click", function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                t.show(++t.index);
            }).addEvent("mouseup", function(){ this.blur(); });
            t.show(0);
            //是否自动播放
            if ( $(elem).attr("class").indexOf("mod-scroll-auto") != -1 ){
                window.setInterval(function(){t.show(++t.index);} , 6000);
            }
            //是否自动播放
        }
        Scrl.prototype = {
            show: function(i){
                var t = this;
                t.index = i < 0 ? t._len - 1 : i > t._len - 1 ? 0 : i;
                t._scrl.onStart = function(){
                    t._ctrls.removeCss("current");
                    t._ctrls.$(t.index).addCss("current");
                    if(t._ctrls_img.length > 0){
                        t._ctrls_img.removeCss("current");
                        t._ctrls_img.$(t.index).addCss("current");
                    }
                }
                t._scrl.scrollTo(t._step * t.index);
            }
        }
        $("div.widget-slide").each(function(){
            new Scrl(this);
        });
        //Mod Scroll
    });
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
    function newsScroll(newslst,inc,delay){
        var _Ntes_Marquee = function(body, direction, fps, lpf) {
            if (!arguments.length) {
                return;
            }
            var t = this;
            t.constructor = arguments.callee;
            // 创建不间断滚动所需的DOM结构
            t._body = body; t._wrapper = body.parentNode;
            t._copy = document.createElement(body.tagName); t._copy.className = body.className; t._copy.innerHTML = body.innerHTML;
            t._wrapper.appendChild(t._copy);
            t._wrapper = t._wrapper.parentNode;
            direction = direction ? direction.toLowerCase() : "left";
            t.setDirection(direction);
            t.fps = isNaN(fps) ? 15 : fps;
            t.lpf = isNaN(lpf) ? 1 : lpf;
            t._timerIds = [];
        };
        _Ntes_Marquee.prototype = {
            setDirection : function(direction) {
                this.move = scrollMode[direction];
                if (!this.move) {
                    throw "not such direction";
                }
            },
            _scroll : function(params) {
                var t = this, lpf = t.lpf;
                if (!t._isPause) {
                    if (params.length !== 0) {
                        if (params.length > 0) {
                            lpf = Math.min(params.length, lpf);
                            params.length -= lpf;
                        }
                        t.move(lpf);
                    } else {
                        t.stop();
                        params.callback && params.callback();
                    }
                }
            },
            start : function() {
                var t = this;
                if (0 === t._timerIds.length) {
                    var length, direction, callback, args = arguments;
                    // 重载
                    switch (typeof args[0]) {
                        case "number":
                            length = args[0];
                            if ("string" === typeof args[1]) {
                                direction = args[1];
                                callback = args[2];
                            } else {
                                callback = args[1];
                            }
                            break;
                        case "string":
                            direction = args[0];
                            length = args[1];
                            callback = args[2];
                            break;
                    }
                    direction && t.setDirection(direction);
                    var params = {
                        length : isNaN(length) ? -1 : parseInt(length)
                    };
                    if (params.length > 0) {
                        params.callback = NTES.util.isFunction(callback) ? callback : undefined;
                    }
                    t._currentScroll = t._scroll.bind(t, params);
                    t._timerIds.push(setInterval(t._currentScroll, t.fps));
                }
            },
            stop : function() {
                var t = this;
                while (t._timerIds.length) {
                    clearInterval(t._timerIds.pop());
                }
                t._currentScroll = undefined;
            },
            speedUp : function() {
                var t = this;
                t._timerIds.length && t._timerIds.push(setInterval(t._currentScroll, t.fps));
            },
            slowDown : function() {
                this._timerIds.length > 1 && clearInterval(this._timerIds.pop());
            },
            go : function() {
                this._isPause = false;
            },
            stay : function() {
                this._isPause = true;
            }
        };
        var scrollMode = {
            // 向左滚动
            left : function(lpf) {
                var t = this;
                t._wrapper.scrollLeft += lpf;
                if (t._copy.offsetWidth - t._wrapper.scrollLeft <= 0) {
                    t._wrapper.scrollLeft -= t._body.offsetWidth;
                }
            },
            // 向右滚动
            right : function(lpf) {
                var t = this, nextValue;
                if (t._wrapper.scrollLeft <= 0) {
                    t._wrapper.scrollLeft += t._body.offsetWidth;
                }
                nextValue = t._wrapper.scrollLeft - lpf;
                t._wrapper.scrollLeft = nextValue < 0 ? t._body.offsetWidth + nextValue : nextValue;
            },
            // 向上滚动
            top : function(lpf) {
                var t = this;
                t._wrapper.scrollTop += lpf;
                if (t._copy.offsetHeight - t._wrapper.scrollTop <= 0) {
                    t._wrapper.scrollTop -= t._body.offsetHeight;
                }
            },
            // 向下滚动
            bottom : function(lpf) {
                var t = this, nextValue;
                if (t._wrapper.scrollTop <= 0) {
                    t._wrapper.scrollTop += t._body.offsetHeight;
                }
                nextValue = t._wrapper.scrollTop - lpf;
                t._wrapper.scrollTop = nextValue < 0 ? t._body.offsetHeight + nextValue : nextValue;
            }
        };
        var suggest_lst = new _Ntes_Marquee(newslst,"top",5);
        window.setInterval(function(){ suggest_lst.start(inc,"top");},delay);
    }
    newsScroll(NTES("#important-news ul")[0],28,4000);
    //]]>
</script>
